from 'prosemirror-state'\nimport { Decoration, DecorationSet } from 'prosemirror-view'\n\n/**\n * Detect @ mention at cursor position by scanning real ProseMirror positions.\n * This avoids string-index to doc-position conversion bugs around hard breaks.\n */\nexport function getMentionStateAtSelection(selection: TextSelection): MentionState {\n    if (!selection.empty) {\n        return null\n    }\n\n    const { doc } = selection.$from\n    const cursorPos = selection.from\n    let mentionFrom: number | null = null\n    let query = ''\n\n    for (let pos = cursorPos; pos > 0; pos--) {\n        const prevPos = pos - 1\n        const char = doc.textBetween(prevPos, pos, '\\n', '\\n')\n\n        if (char === '\\n') {\n            break\n        }\n\n        if (char === '@') {\n            mentionFrom = prevPos\n            break\n        }\n\n        if (char) {\n            query = char + query\n            continue\n        }\n\n        // Stop at text block boundaries (e.g., paragraph splits).\n        const prevParent = doc.resolve(prevPos).parent\n        const currParent = doc.resolve(pos).parent\n        if (prevParent !== currParent) {\n            break\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (mentionFrom === null) {\n        return null\n    }\n\n    return {\n        active: true,\n        from: mentionFrom,\n        to: cursorPos,\n        query,\n    }\n}\n\n// Coords type for ProseMirror coordsAtPos\ntype Coords = { left: number; right: number; top: number; bottom: number }\n\n// Use basic ProseMirror schema directly\nexport const editorSchema = basicSchema\n\n// new PluginKey<MentionState>('mention')\n\n// Mention detection plugin\nexport function mentionPlugin(opts: { onChange: (state: MentionState, coords?: Coords) => void }): Plugin {\n    return new Plugin<MentionState>({\n        key: mentionKey,\n        state: {\n            init: (): MentionState => null,\n            apply(tr, prev, _oldState, newState): MentionState {\n                const sel = newState.selection as TextSelection\n                if (!sel.empty) return null // Only handle cursor selection\n\n                return getMentionStateAtSelection(sel)\n            },\n        },\n\n        props: {\n            decorations(state) {\n                const mention = mentionKey.getState(state)\n                if (!mention || !mention.active) return null\n\n                return DecorationSet.create(state.doc, [\n                    Decoration.inline(mention.from, mention.to, {\n                        class: 'pm-mention-active',\n                    }),\n                ])\n            },\n        },\n\n        view(editorView) {\n            // Check initial state immediately when view is created\n            const initialState =      try {\n                    const domCoords = editorView.coordsAtPos(initialState.from) as Coords\n                    opts.onChange(initialState, domCoords)\n                } catch (e) {\n                    // In test environment, coordsAtPos might fail - call onChange without coordinates\n                    opts.onChange(initialState, undefined)\n                }\n            }\n\n            return {\n                update(view, prevState) {\n                    const prev = mentionKey.getState(prevState)\n                    const curr = mentionKey.getState(view.state)\n\n                    // Only trigger onChange if state actually changed\n                    if (prev === curr) {\n                        return\n                    }\n\n                    if (curr && curr.active) {\n                        // Get coordinates for the \"@\" character position (from), not cursor (to)\n                        try {\n                            const domCoords = opts.onChange(null)\n                    }\n                },\n            }\n        },\n    })\n}\n\n// Helper function to apply suggestion selection\nexport function applySuggestion(view: any, suggestion: string) {\n    const mentionState = mentionKey.getState(view.state)\n    if (!mentionState) return\n\n    const { from, to } = mentionState\n    const docSize = view.state.doc.content.size\n    const newText = suggestion + ' '\n\n    // Safety check: ensure positions are within document bounds\n    if (from < 0 || to > docSize || from > to) {\n        console.warn('Invalid mention position range:', { from, to, docSize })\n        return\n    }\n\n    // Guard against stale mention state. Only replace when the range still starts at '@'.\n    if (from + 1 > docSize || view.state.doc.textBetween(from, from + 1, '\\n', '\\n') !== '@') {\n        console.warn('Ignoring stale mention range:', { from, to, docSize })\n        return\n    }\n\n    const tr = view.state.tr.insertText(newText, from, to)\n    const newPos = Math.min(from + newText.length, tr.doc.content.size)\n\n    view.dispatch(tr.setSelection(TextSelection.create(tr.doc, newPos)))\n    view.focus()\n}\n\n// Suggestion interaction interface for keyboard plugin\ninterface SuggestionInteraction {\n onSubmit?: () => void\n    disabled?: () => boolean\n    getValue?: () => string\n    getSuggestionState?: () => SuggestionInteraction | null\n    onOpenImagePicker?: () => void\n}): Plugin {\n if (suggestionState && suggestionState.suggestions.length > 0) {\n                suggestionState.navigateSelection('down')\n                return true // Handled\n            }\n            return      },\n\n        // Handle Enter key for suggestion selection OR form submission\n        Enter: (state, dispatch, view) => {\n            const suggestionState = opts.getSuggestionState?.()\n\n            // If suggestions are active, select the current suggestion\n            if (suggestionState && suggestionState.suggestions.length > 0) {\n                const currentSuggestion = suggestionState.suggestions[suggestionState.selectedIndex]\n                if (currentSuggestion) {\n                    suggestionState.selectSuggestion(currentSuggestion)\n value?.trim() && opts.onSubmit) {\n                opts.onSubmit()\n                return true // Handled\n            }\n\n            return false // Let ProseMirror handle (will create new line)\n        },\n\n        // Handle Tab key for suggestion selection\n        Tab: (state, dispatch, view) => {\n            const suggestionState = opts.getSuggestionState?.()\n\n            // If suggestions are active, select the current suggestion with Tab\n            if (suggestionState && suggestionState.suggestions.length > 0) {\n                const currentSuggestion = suggestionState.suggestions[suggestionState.selectedIndex]\n                if (currentSuggestion) {\n                    suggestionState.selectSuggestion(currentSuggestion)\n                    return true // Handled\n                }\n            }\n\n            return false // Let ProseMirror handle default Tab behavior\n        },\n\n        // Handle Shift+Enter for explicit newlines\n        'Shift-Enter': (state, dispatch, view) => {\n            // Use ProseMirror's built-in hard break insertion to properly handle cursor positioning\n            const { hard_break } = state.schema.nodes\n            if (!hard_break || !dispatch) {\n                return false\n            }\n\n            const tr = state.tr.replaceSelectionWith(hard_break.create())\n            dispatch(tr)\n            return true // Prevent submit logic\n        },\n\n        // Handle Escape to close suggestions\n        Escape: (state, dispatch, view) => {\n            // Check if we're                return false // Not in mention mode, let ProseMirror handle\n            }\n\n            // Hide suggestions if they're showing\n            const suggestionState = current cursor position)\n            // This works whether suggestions are showing or not\n            if (dispatch) {\n                const tr = state.tr.delete(pmMention.from, pmMention.to)\n                dispatch(tr)\n            }\n\n            return true // Handled\n        },\n    })\n}\n\nexport interface ImagePluginCallbacks {\n    onFiles: (files: File[]) => void\n}\n\nexport function imagePlugin(callbacks: ImagePluginCallbacks): Plugin {\n    return new Plugin({\n        props: {\n            handlePaste: (_view, event) => {\n                const clipboard = (event as }\n\n                if (files.length > 0) {\n                    event.preventDefault()\n                    callbacks.onFiles(files)\n                    return true\n                }\n\n                return false\n            },\n\n            handleDrop: (_view, event) => {\n                const dataTransfer = (event as DragEvent).dataTransfer\n                if (!dataTransfer ||                     frag.content\n                            .map(node => {\n                                if (node.type.name === 'image') {\n                                    return null\n
